The letter to the Yunnan Construction Department is recorded as follows: "Sir, it has been found that copper is one of the main raw materials for heavy industry. It is especially a necessary raw material for the electrical manufacturing industry. In recent years, China's electrical products have been thriving. However, due to the lack of copper mining in the country, the raw materials still need to be imported from abroad, and profits are inevitably lost, which is regrettable. In view of this, our association has decided to suggest to the government to conduct mining. A mine source has now been found near Huangshigang. However, the various plans regarding the suggestion must be widely adopted and thoroughly researched in order to be comprehensive. It is heard that your department already has copper mining in Yunnan and has achieved considerable results. Therefore, we dare to send a letter to inquire. Please kindly provide guidance, detailing the actual amount of your mine, the mining period, the sales location, and future facilities, so that we can learn from it and facilitate progress. We will be publicly grateful."

The Mechanical Industry Association Assists Factories in Automatically Inspecting Safety Equipment Zhang Zhongjie Talks About the Importance of Industrial Safety 129

According to the Central News Agency, the issue of factory inspection has been actively carried out by the authorities and has achieved considerable results. The city is full of factories. Although it has been successfully carried out in the urban area, the issue of factory inspection in the concession has not been effectively handled. It is now initiated by the Mechanical Industry Association to automatically inspect the safety equipment of factories. The association has stipulated the automatic inspection method and distributed it to factories for implementation, and has hired industrial safety expert Zhang Zhongjie to assist in the implementation. According to Mr. Zhang's opinions on industrial safety issues, in recent years, some unfortunate events have occurred in national goods factories, which have attracted the attention of the authorities in the Chinese and Concessions, and there have been factory inspections. The Ministry of Industry of our country has specially set up a Central Factory Inspection Office, and on January 21 this year, it held an industrial safety and health exhibition in Beijing. Therefore, the issue of factory safety equipment has been taken seriously by the general public. The main points of inspecting factories are nothing more than hygiene equipment, fire prevention equipment, and the situation of mechanical equipment, etc., and special attention is paid to fire prevention equipment. In fact, hygiene and safety equipment should also be included in the industrial development plan in scientific management, because the health of workers is also the health of productivity, and safety devices are also the safety guarantee of capital and the foundation of business development. Therefore, factories in Europe and the United States do not neglect any safety measures, but my country's industry is suppressed by industrially advanced countries, and there is no room for development. Therefore, the establishment and facilities of general national goods factories are struggling in hardship. Capital and talent are lacking. Since capital is short, equipment has to be simple. Since talent is lacking, it is not known how to improve its facilities. Therefore, we hope that the authorities will take into account the difficulties of the lack of capital and talent in national goods factories, and should not start from the negative mandatory relocation and closure of factories, but should assist in the positive design and planning. There are two ways for the national goods industry to plan hygiene and safety equipment. One is for various national goods factories to jointly hire experts with this kind of specialized knowledge to stipulate this plan, and the other is to negotiate with manufacturers of safe industrial products to make the most economical safety settings. Therefore, on the one hand, the authorities should understand the difficulties of the business, so that the inspection is not suppression but assistance, and on the other hand, the factories should take the initiative to discuss and work hard for safety issues. Now the Shanghai Mechanical Industry Association has regulations for the automatic inspection of factory safety equipment, and it is hoped that the industrial community can take it seriously. In the future, the results will naturally be effective.

China and Foreign Famine Relief Association Plans to Dredge the Quanhe River in Shandong 131

The China and Foreign Famine Relief Association at No. 505 Henan Road has always adhered to the purpose of building and relieving disasters. The huge projects that have been held over the years, such as the Lijin Dam in Shandong, the Shishou Dam in Hubei, the Qianli Dam and Dacheng Ditch in Hebei, the Shilushui Canal, the Minsheng Canal in Suiyuan, the Jinghui Canal and the West-Lan Highway in Shaanxi, and other well-drilling and river-dredging projects, either repaired, built, or jointly organized with the government, are all measures to benefit the country and the people and have achieved considerable results. Recently, in response to the request of the Magistrate of Wenshang County, Shandong, the association has undertaken to dredge the Quanhe River and has sent Mr. Zhang Jichun, the chief engineer of the association's engineering department, to inspect. It is said that the Quanhe River originates from the mountain springs northeast of Wenshang County and flows into Shushan Lake southwest of the county seat, with a total length of 80 li. Every summer flood season, the water level rises sharply, the river is rapid, and the disaster of flooding is inevitable every year. The victims, calculated along 170 villages along the river, are no less than 40,000. The loss of agricultural products is about 800,000 yuan per year. The dredging plan requires 1.6 million cubic meters of mud for embankment construction. In addition to the dredging of the river, it is planned to collect mud from nearby. If 10,000 workers are hired every day, it will take 80 days to complete. The wages for each person per day, calculated at 20 cents in national currency, will cost 160,000 yuan. The county government, hindered by funds, in addition to recruiting 8,500 workers locally to engage in work, the remaining 1,500 people will be recruited from neighboring counties. The required wages of 24,000 yuan, and the cost of tools and supervisors, about 3,000 yuan, are requested to be borne by the China and Foreign Famine Relief Association. It is heard that the plan has been submitted to the Executive Committee of the association for discussion, and once the decision is made, construction will begin on a selected day.

This City's Judicial Authorities Take the First Step in Promoting the Notary System 133

Various Regulations Are Being Submitted to the Central Political Council for Review

Da Gong She [大公社] reports that the judicial administration department [司法行政部], following the precedents of European and American countries, is preparing to implement the notary system. The judicial authorities of this city, in order to promote this notary system, have formulated regulations, including (1) Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Provisional Notary Rules [公證暫行規則施行細則], (2) Notary Fee Rules [公證費用規則], and 25 other types of thin books, booklets and forms. Once the various regulations are successively approved and promulgated, the judicial organs of this city will be the first to conduct trials. In the future, the parties applying for notary matters will need to have the following main procedures ready with the court: (1) creating a notarized document (created by the court based on the party's application), (2) authenticating private documents (created by private individuals and authenticated by the court). The advantage of the notary system is that all public and private contracts and agreements, once a notarized document is created, or a private document is legally recognized by the court, its legally binding force is stronger than ordinary contracts. Because according to the proposed provisional rules, it is stipulated that all notarized documents related to monetary compensation in civil lawsuits shall state that in the event of forced execution of the case, the parties may directly request the court for execution without court adjudication. Therefore, from this point alone, its general effectiveness can be imagined.

Arriving at the Wharf of Kung Ho Hsiang [公和祥] at 1 PM; Open for Visits Today and Tomorrow; Leaving Shanghai Early

If various circles wish to visit, they can send a letter to the agency to request tickets (but it must be in the name of a merchant; individual personal tickets will not be issued). The steamer is scheduled to leave Shanghai the day after tomorrow (Sunday) at 10 AM, heading to Yokohama and Kobe in Japan. It will then return to Germany on the 19th with passengers from Shanghai on the 16th for its maiden voyage.

The French Municipal Council Restricts the Gong Ming [公明] Factory from Increasing the Number of Workers 135

Only 70 People Are Allowed to Remain; Otherwise, Closure Will Be Ordered

Xin Sheng She [新聲社] reports that the Gong Ming [公明] Electric Bulb Factory at No. 4, Hexing Lane [和興里], in the French Concession, has been open for eight years, registered with the Social Affairs Bureau [社會局], and obtained a license from the French Municipal Council. It is a well-known national electric bulb manufacturer. Because the original workers were insufficient, they successively increased the number of workers and expanded the factory site. Unexpectedly, it was repeatedly interfered with and punished by the French Municipal Council. The factory painfully paid the fines, thinking that it would be fine, but on the 27th of last month, the Municipal Council, together with the Health Department and the Fire Department, sent personnel to claim that only 70 people were allowed to work; otherwise, the business would be ordered to close by the 5th of this month. The police even sent a fire truck to the factory and used a hose to spray water to force it to stop working, causing the factory to suffer great losses. Now, the factory, unable to withstand the oppression, has reported the situation to the Electric Appliance Manufacturing Industry Association [電器製造業同業公會] for relief. It is heard that the association, in order to protect the rights of its members, and because the Ministry of Industry is now paying attention to national goods factories, and the Social Affairs Bureau is doing its best to protect registered factories, plans to submit a petition to higher-level authorities to forcefully argue with the French Concession authorities.

The Cattle and Sheep Industry Association Discussed Opposition to the Border Crossing Tax Yesterday 138

Three Measures Were Agreed Upon; Continued Request for Negotiations

The French Concession Public Works Bureau [法租界公董局] recently enacted a new cattle and sheep border crossing tax, which came into effect in January 1936. The Shanghai Cattle and Sheep Industry Association [上海市牛淩晨業同業公會] listed various reasons why the border crossing tax was unreasonable in a letter to the French Public Works Bureau last month, requesting its cancellation. Now, the French Public Works Bureau has replied, stating that it cannot be cancelled. More than one hundred companies of the entire industry have jointly requested the association to find a way to deal with it. After receiving the letter, the association believed that the French Concession Public Works Bureau's newly added exorbitant taxes and levies were indeed unreasonable and had a great impact on the livelihoods of the entire industry. Therefore, it convened a meeting of all employees at 3 PM on the 7th of this month, presided over by Chen Guanghai [陳廣海], the chairman of the association. Three measures were agreed upon: (1) Continue to request the Municipal Chamber of Commerce [市商會], the Municipal Government [市政府], and the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession [法租界納稅華人會] to negotiate with the Director of the French Public Works Bureau to quickly cancel the tax. (2) Notify the entire industry to temporarily suspend the transportation of cattle and sheep through the French Concession until the case is satisfactorily resolved. (3) If the French Concession authorities insist on acting arbitrarily, unite the entire industry and unanimously refuse to slaughter cattle and sheep at the slaughterhouse in the French Concession and refuse to purchase the post-slaughter inspection tickets that the Public Works Bureau requires each beef shop to pre-purchase each month. The meeting adjourned at 6 PM.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Explains That Receipts and Insurance Policies Do Not Need to Be Stamped 139

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce [上海市商會] sent a letter to the Asia Petroleum Company [亞洲火油公司] yesterday to explain that insurance receipts do not need to be stamped, stating: "The insurance policy is a certificate of rights and can only be considered as a future financial relationship, not a current financial income. Article 16, Section 2 of the Stamp Tax Law only states that any receipt issued after receiving money belongs to the category of money receipts, and does not say that any receipt issued after receiving a future financial relationship belongs to the scope of money receipts. Therefore, this association believes that the receipt issued after receiving the insurance policy does not belong to the scope of money receipts and does not need to be stamped."

The China Flying Club [中國飛行社] Holds Free Sightseeing Flights 149

The China Flying Club [中國飛行社], organized by the China Aviation Association [中國航空協會], has been working actively since its establishment. People in the country have joined one after another. Recently, in various parts of Southeast Asia, there has also been a surge of interest. "For example, in the corner of the Philippines, as many as 20 members joined on the same day. Other ports are registering one after another, not including them. The club is currently building an airport and adding aircraft. Once everything is complete, it will officially open classes and hold flight training. Before the classes are opened, in order to promote the atmosphere, promote interest, and become accustomed to aerial movements, the latest training aircraft will be used to hold sightseeing flights and offer free opportunities to attract people. It is expected that those who register at that time will be even more enthusiastic. The club's temporary measures for sightseeing flights are recorded below: Temporary Measures for Free Sightseeing Flights in Shanghai Held by the China Flying Club [中國飛行社]: (1) This club is holding sightseeing flights to promote the social atmosphere, promote interest in flight, and become accustomed to aerial movements, tentatively for two months. (2) Before the official opening of the flight class, new training aircraft will be used to hold sightseeing flights so that members and young people interested in aviation can have the opportunity to participate first. (3) Those who participate in the sightseeing flights will not be charged, but must comply with the following items: (A) Participants are not divided by gender. If they are physically strong, they are limited to those who are suitable for flying. The registration period is from February 10th to February 25th of this year. (B) Round-trip to the airport will be provided by the club's special car. (C) Members of the China Aviation Association [中國航空協會] and members of this club who participate will be charged a car fee of two yuan, which will be paid at the time of registration. (D) Those who are not members of the Aviation Association and members of this club but want to participate will also be charged a car fee of two yuan, but must also join this club as members at the same time to enjoy all the rights of members. (E) It is held once every Wednesday, Saturday, and Sunday. (F) Flight suits are provided by this club. (G) Participants must follow the scheduled order to ride and abide by the various rules of the airfield. (H) Those who register will first be assigned to sightseeing shifts and dates by this club, and will be notified one day in advance. They must arrive at the club 15 minutes before the scheduled time to go to the airfield together. If they do not arrive at the time, the sightseeing certificate will be invalidated and will not be rescheduled for the next flight. (4) Participants can register directly at the club's office at No. 1, Luban Lane [呂班坊], Route Tenant de May [呂班路], French Concession.

The Shanghai Telephone Company [上海電話公司] sent a notice to all telephone users yesterday, stating: "The Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement [上海公共租界工部局] and the French Municipal Council [法租界工董局] have approved the company's revised telephone tariff regulations, which will take effect on March 1st of this year. This new chapter is revised according to the charging method of calls. Therefore, from March 1st, the general telephone tariff will be calculated according to the number of calls. The calculation method is listed as follows: The number of calls owed by the user is recorded by the motor. Each line has a counter, which is extremely accurate. The recording method of this table is that the call is recorded on the counter of the caller only after the two lines of the caller and the receiver are connected and an echo is received. The table of the receiver will never record. Furthermore, if the dialed phone is busy with another call, or has been connected but there is no echo, the call will not be recorded. Calls to the company's departments (94090), the telephone number inquiry office (09), the repair office (01), emergency calls (00), etc., are not recorded. As for the dedicated lines for commercial use and the outdoor machine lines, they are not included in the above tariffs. The separate table is as follows. The details of the application of the new tariff and other miscellaneous fees will be notified to each user separately. The new tariff and detailed regulations will be printed out soon and displayed in the company's business department for users to refer to and review. Charging method: The company's billing date and method for telephone calls in various districts of this city will still follow the previous example in the February period, but from March 1st, all telephone bills in each district will be calculated in accordance with the new regulations and prepaid from the monthly billing date (monthly fee). The number of local calls exceeding the quota in that month will be calculated until three days before the billing date of the following month. The total number will be calculated at three cents per call and included in the following month's bill. Border calls are also calculated in this way. The Shanghai Telephone Company [電話公司] announcement."

Hazy Weather Followed by Snow; Farmers Generally Hold Hidden Worries

Since the entry of the Spring Equinox [立春節] on the 5th, the weather in this city has been extremely hazy, and the air pressure is also low, making it unstable. However, farmers are worried that because it is spring snow, it may inevitably affect crops in the future.

The Case of Two Western Police Officers Deliberately Killing a Chinese Man; Continued Interrogation of Witnesses Yesterday 150

Lawyer Questions Witness on Private Matters; Shen Jinsheng [沈金生] Reads Out English Words

The case of Western Inspector Peter and Probationary Inspector Gigert [巨特] of the Jiaxing Road [嘉興路] Police Station, accused of deliberately killing Chinese man Ma Debiao [馬德標], was tried for the fourth time yesterday morning by the British Court for China [駐華英國法院]. Doctors and nurses from the Tongren Hospital [同仁醫院] were summoned, all proving that Ma Debiao [馬德標] was wet all over when he was sent to the hospital by ambulance that day. Also, during the interrogation on the afternoon of the previous day, the witness, vegetable vendor Shen Jinsheng [沈金生] (transliteration), who rescued Ma Debiao [馬德標] from the water on the day, was repeatedly questioned by the defendant's lawyers, Ricks [里克斯] and McDonald [麥唐納], and accused of being a rogue and a procurer. Shen immediately denied it and asked the lawyers to provide evidence that he was a rogue and a procurer. Ricks [里克斯] then asked Shen if he lived in a brothel. Shen replied that he was in court to testify, and the lawyer was involving his private matters. Ricks [里克斯] then asked Shen if he had been imprisoned. Shen replied that he had only been detained for smoking opium. McDonald [麥唐納] asked Shen if he dared to swear that he was not a procurer. Shen replied that he was not a procurer. Although there was a brothel in his house, it was a cohabitant and had nothing to do with him. One of the jurors asked Shen if he could recognize English numbers. Shen replied that he could. The juror then wrote the four characters 7043 on a large card and held it up to show him. Shen read it out without hesitation. More than 20 witnesses have been summoned in this case in recent days, and there are still a few others. It is expected that all of them can be interrogated in one or two days, and then the argument will begin.

Yi Feng Enamel Factory Manager Wu Huangxiang's Home Robbed 153

Three Thieves Knocked, Falsely Claiming Matters at the Factory, Searched and Plundered Valuables, Escaped, Then Reported to Police for Investigation

Wu Huangxiang, 30 years old, from Anhui, resident of No. 13 Jidouli, Xietu Road, Nanshi, is the manager of Yi Feng Enamel Factory, and his business is quite prosperous. However, he was coveted by bandits. Yesterday morning around 7 o'clock, three bandits, speaking in local and Jiangbei accents, one wearing a blue cloth long gown, and two wearing blue cloth short jackets, knocked on the back door, falsely claiming important matters at the factory. At the time, Wu Huangxiang and his wife were still in bed, only the maid was in the living room washing the faces of two girls. She went to open the door, and the bandits rushed in. One bandit guarded downstairs, and two bandits, holding guns, went upstairs to watch over Mr. and Mrs. Wu, and searched and plundered extensively. They robbed cash of 100 yuan, small coins of 200 jiao, a gold woman's wristwatch, a gold pocket watch, a gold ring, a gemstone ring, and a small diamond ring, one of each, two pairs of gold earrings, more than 200 pieces of small pearls, and also Wu's privately owned six-inch Pibei pistol (gun number 6338, gun license 0784), and 50 bullets. The entire process took about two hours (from 7 a.m. to 9 a.m.). The bandit downstairs suspected something and went upstairs to peek. At this time, the maid took the opportunity to slip into the living room of No. 14, went out the back door, and loudly shouted "Catch the thieves!" The bandits heard the sound and escaped through the back door without a trace. Afterward, the victim reported to the Liyuan Road Police Station, which reported to the Ximen Branch. Branch Chief Yao ordered Detective Squad Leader Li Xiaobao and Detective Zhao Renxin to go to investigate and start the investigation.

Three Criminals Passing Themselves Off As Military Officers Arrested In An Apartment On Avenue Joffre 154

Three Criminals Served As Brigade Commander, Secretary, and Staff Officer, Defrauding For Money; Gang Members Arrested in Hankou, Leading to the Crackdown in Shanghai

Wang Dongyu, 25 years old, from Shangyu, Zhejiang; Zhang Xueli, 20 years old, from the same town as Wang; and Yu Hou, 24 years old, from Longyou, Zhejiang, falsely claimed to be officers of the 5th Brigade, 2nd Column, of the Northern Sichuan Guerrilla Force of the Xiang, E, and Chuan Border剿匪軍. Wang pretended to be the brigade commander, Zhang the secretary, and Yu the staff officer. Recently, they opened Room 27 in the apartment at No. 66 Avenue Bugeaud, Avenue Joffre, in the French Concession, organized a fake headquarters, wantonly issued letters of appointment and symbols, sold official positions and titles, and defrauded people for money. They also sent their gang members Yu Lei, Wang Ziqi, and 15 others to Hankou to carry out fraudulent activities in secret. On the evening of a certain day, Li, the battalion commander of the Wuhan Garrison Command Military Police Battalion, and others arrested Yu, Wang, and the other 15 people, and seized fake evidence documents, which were sent to the Military Law Office of the Wuhan Garrison Command for investigation. They confessed to the location of the headquarters in Shanghai, and that Wang or Yu was the brigade commander, Huang Shangmei the staff officer, and Yu Hou the quartermaster, etc. According to the confession, the Wuhan Garrison Command telegraphed the Shanghai Songhu Garrison, which immediately ordered the Detective Team Inspector Yang Fengqi and Xu Pengfei to report to the French Concession Police and request assistance the day before yesterday afternoon. They rushed to Room 27 of the Avenue Joffre apartment and arrested Wang Dongyu, Zhang Xueli, and Yu Hou. Wang and Yu were wearing plain clothes, while Zhang was wearing a military uniform and hat. They also seized forged official documents, symbols, letters of appointment, seals, etc., all packed in a suitcase, and brought them back to the police station. According to Wang's confession, he had never been in the military before. This time, he was ordered by the fugitive Huang to organize a headquarters and raise military funds in Shanghai to be transported to the front lines. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District, where Judge Li Changnian conducted a preliminary hearing. Attorney Fei Xizhen of the Police Department stated the case, briefly saying that the defendants were arrested by the Police Department with the assistance of the Garrison Command for impersonating military officers. Because the Police Department still needed to investigate whether the defendants had committed any crimes in the concession, he requested an adjournment for further questioning. The investigating detective also reported on the process of assisting in the arrest of the defendants and presented the seized evidence. Subsequently, Yang Fengqi, the inspector of the Shanghai Songhu Garrison Command, submitted a document to the court, requesting permission to transfer the three defendants so that they could be sent back to Wuhan for trial. Questioned the defendants confessed to serving as military officers, unknowingly untruthful, as a result of the fugitive Huang family’s duplicity. The court verified the confession and ordered a second hearing on the 14th, and the defendants were returned to custody.

False Telephone Report of Jailbreak 155

Detectives Rushed, Found Nothing; Source of Call Under Investigation

The Central Police Station of Lokawei in the French Concession received a telephone report at 2:45 p.m. yesterday, stating that prisoners in the Second Special District Prison on Route Massenet were attempting to escape, causing a commotion, and requesting that detectives be sent to suppress it. The captain led Chinese, Western, and Vietnamese detectives to investigate inside the prison, only to find that no prisoners were trying to escape or causing any disturbances. Everything was peaceful as usual. The captain led the detectives back to the police station to investigate the source of the telephone call for further action.

Young Man Writes Eleven Suicide Notes, Then Poisons Himself 156

Corpse Examined By Court Yesterday

Li Jiaju, also known as Haibao, a young man from Ningbo, around 20 years old, recently became unemployed and despondent, leading him to contemplate suicide. On the afternoon of the 5th, at 5 p.m., he bought raw opium and opened Room 29 at the Chunjiang Second Inn, No. 315 Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession. He ordered the room attendant to bring writing tools and wrote as many as eleven suicide notes, addressed to his parents, maternal uncle, friends, etc., and to the inn, stating the reasons for his suicide. After finishing writing, he swallowed the raw opium, lay down on the bed, and waited for death to arrive. At 3 a.m. that night, he groaned in pain due to the poison. The room attendant, Chen Heshang (43 years old, local), discovered him and reported to the accountant, who immediately hired a car to send Li to Renji Hospital for treatment. He also reported to the French Concession Police, who dispatched Detective Wu Wengang to investigate. However, because he was deeply poisoned, the treatment was ineffective. He died at 11 a.m. the next morning. The hospital reported to the police station, which sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-hall for examination. The detective summoned the deceased's maternal uncle, Zhu Xiangding (resident of No. 36 Ning'an Lane, Haining Road), to the case. Yesterday morning, the Second Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Wang Ren and a forensic medical secretary to the site to determine that the deceased had indeed died from poisoning himself. They took their seats in the courtroom, and Detective Zhang Chunsheng reported on the investigation process and presented the deceased's suicide notes. The official questioned the witnesses Chen Heshang and the relative of the deceased, Zhu Xiangding, and examined the suicide notes. He then ordered that the body be released to Zhu Xiangding for burial and that the suicide notes also be given to Zhu.

As a result, Yang Shaopeng was returned to custody to await further instructions.

Detailed Account of Robbery on Shujin Lane 158

According to Municipal Council news, at approximately 7:40 PM on January 20th, Fudan female student Hu Peihuan was walking from west to east on Nanjing Road near the south side of the road, approximately five yards east of Cifeng Lane. A man approached from behind and snatched her handbag from under Hu's left arm, then escaped southward with another man who had been standing at the entrance of the lane. After passing through Cifeng Lane, the plaintiff shouted loudly that her handbag had been snatched. Thereupon, several pedestrians and Hu chased the escaping defendant. Some people shouted "Catch the robber!" After passing through Cifeng Lane, the robber reached Jiujiang Road and fled into Huajin Lane, continuing south to Hankou Road. During the chase, the second defendant disappeared. As the robber reached Hankou Road, someone blew a police whistle. A large group of people and Hu were chasing him. From Hankou Road, the defendant ran east, and after about ten yards, suddenly turned around and ran west to Shanxi Road. Chinese Constable No. 2211, standing guard at the corner of Hankou Road and Shanxi Road, heard the police whistle and the shouts of "Catch the robber!" He took out his pistol and loaded it, believing that a robbery had occurred. At the same time, the constable was walking east on Hankou Road when he suddenly saw a Chinese man coming from east to west, with his right hand under his short jacket, followed by a crowd. The constable ordered him to stop, but he continued running forward, still keeping his hand under his short jacket. When the man was about five yards away from the constable, he still did not stop, despite the constable repeatedly ordering him to halt. The constable, fearing he was carrying a weapon, fired four shots, hitting him twice. The man fell to the ground on Hankou Road outside No. 359, about thirty yards east of Shanxi Road. When the deceased was caught by Chinese Constable No. 2211, the handbag fell from under his short jacket. The man was immediately sent to Renji Hospital, but was pronounced dead upon arrival. The plaintiff identified the deceased as the person who had robbed her handbag.

Temple Incense Flourishing on Yesterday's Lantern Festival 159

City God Temple and Rainbow Temple Crowded with People, Considerable Incense Revenue Throughout the Day

Yesterday was the Lantern Festival, and the City God Temple in the city and the Rainbow Temple on Nanjing Road were both filled with flourishing incense. From morning to night, the temples were overflowing with worshipers, with a preponderance of lavishly dressed women, adorned with jewels, shimmering accessories, and fragrant clothing, showing extreme elegance. The staff were constantly bowing and prostrating, extremely busy. At the same time, many idle guests lingered in the temple, finding pleasure in mocking others, appearing quite vulgar. According to statistics, the revenue from incense and candles at both temples yesterday was considerable.

Unidentified Man Killed By Bus, Coroner Investigates 160

Efforts to Locate Family Unsuccessful, Body Entrusted to Charitable Hall

The day before yesterday afternoon around 5 p.m., an unidentified man, about thirty years old, wearing a Zhongshan suit with a yellow raincoat over it, a peaked cap, and leather shoes, resembling a worker, was riding a bicycle No. 13289 from west to east on the Xinzha Road Wuzhen Road Bridge. Unexpectedly, a Route 10 bus No. 15006, driven by Li Fusheng, came speeding from the east. Unable to avoid the collision in time, the bus knocked down the bicycle and the man, rolling them both under the right front wheel. Chinese Constable No. 2417 spotted the incident and immediately reported it to the Xinzha Police Station by telephone, which summoned an ambulance. They managed to pull the man and the bicycle out from under the bus, but the man was already severely injured and barely breathing, and the bicycle was completely crushed. The man was rushed to Baolong Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at 1:10 a.m. yesterday morning. Detective Yang Youshan and others from the police station investigated. Because the deceased was unable to speak after being hit, his name and address could not be ascertained. The license plate he was carrying indicated it was from He Dazheng at No. 252 Dalianwan Road, but upon investigation, there was no such address. The body was sent to the Fielun Road Morgue. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Tang and others from the First Special District Court came to the morgue to examine the body. The Western captain reported that the detectives had investigated the scene of the accident and learned that the deceased's bicycle wheel had entered the tram tracks, making it impossible to control, and the front of the bicycle was facing the south bay, causing the collision. He also presented a diagram of the accident scene. Chinese Constable No. 2417 submitted a report on the situation at the time. Mr. Tang then ruled that the unidentified man had been killed by being run over by bus No. 15006. The body was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.

Liang Kehe, Accomplice in Major Post Office Robbery, Continues Trial 161

Liang Denies Conspiracy To Rob, Judgment Postponed For Seven Days

The Major Robbery case at the North Sichuan Road Postal Administration on September 9th last year, in which a huge sum was stolen, eventually led to the arrest of the ringleader Ji Rentang (alias Wukong Monk) from Jiangbei, and accomplices Qiu Guobin, receiver of stolen goods Li Yisheng, and female accomplices Ji Chenshi, Wang Chenshi, and others. They were sent to the First Special District Court for joint trial, and their confessions were clear. Ji Rentang was sentenced to life imprisonment, and the others were sentenced to varying terms, as reported in this newspaper. Later, on December 3rd of last year, the Dithmarschen Road Police went to Luo'an County, Jiangbei, to extradite Liang Kehe (alias Xiaoguangzi, 32 years old) from Che Ning, who was accused of assisting and instigating the robbery. He was sent to court and testified that he had returned to his hometown at that time to deal with land disputes and entrusted a relative surnamed Cha to handle them. However, in Ji Rentang's confession, his maternal uncle Li San also participated in the robbery. He had previously confessed that he and Li San had tea once at the Tiger Stove on Yucai Road in Zhabei. His testimony was very cunning. The person surnamed Cha works in Nanjing. An order was issued to send a letter to the relevant authorities for consultation. Liang Kehe was detained. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Shuzi came to Criminal Court No. 3. An Municipal Council lawyer came to Shanghai from his hometown, selling cloth. He returned to his hometown in July and denied conspiring to rob the post office. He currently does not know the whereabouts of his maternal uncle Li San. He sought judgment. Judge Jiang ruled that he would remain in custody and that the matter would be verified and reviewed again in seven days.

Letters to the Editor 163

Respectfully, I read your newspaper on February 5th, which contained a news item titled "Ministry of Industry and Commerce Asks the Municipal Government to Investigate the Reasons for the Delay in Company Registration," which stated that our bureau has delayed company registration cases, and that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has asked the Municipal Government to investigate the reasons. After investigation, our bureau has handled thousands of company registration cases. In the past, due to special reasons, some cases were delayed. We have already submitted the reasons for the delay to the Municipal Government's Directive No. 17216, which approved the transfer to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. Fearing that the truth is unclear, it is inevitable to confuse the hearing. We hereby send a letter for your review and hope that you will publish the original letter to show the truth. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, February 7th.

Respectfully, yesterday I saw in your newspaper on the 6th of this month, the Nanjing telegraphic news regarding the outcome of the Western doctors' petition. The news contained is slightly inconsistent with the facts. Please make the following corrections: "A. At 10:00 am on the 5th of this month, Qian Longzhang, the representative of the petitioning representatives from various provinces, cities, and counties of our association, met with Weng Wenhao, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and proposed two key points of the petition: (1) Those who practice medicine before the promulgation of the Western Medical Regulations in the 18th year and have variable qualifications, shall be issued a medical practice license. (2) Those who practice medicine after the 18th year, shall be issued a three-year medical assistant license, which shall be exchanged for a medical practice certificate upon expiration. It was approved to transfer the establishment method for improvement and promulgation. Here is a correction. Please write safely. The Secretariat of the Chinese Western Medical Association, February 7th.

Municipal Council Fire Brigade Annual Report for Last Year

Total of 791 Departures Throughout the Year, 47 Lives Lost

The Fire Department of the Municipal Council's 1935 annual report states that the fire brigade departed a total of 791 times for fires and special events this year, a decrease of 209 times compared to the previous year. 47 civilians died in fires, and 5 died in special accidents. The value of property endangered by fire totaled over 115.49 million yuan, an increase of over 30 million yuan compared to the previous year. The actual loss was over 1.534 million yuan, an increase of over 625,000 yuan compared to the previous year. Furthermore, the fire brigade was requested to extinguish fires outside the boundary a total of 36 times this year. For water firefighting, a total of six ships and one barge were rescued. The major fire incidents that can be recorded this year include the two accidental incidents at the Da Zhonghua Baolu Toy Factory on Xiaoshadu Road, in which 27 people died and 62 were injured. Also, the fire at the Denglu Cargo Warehouse at No. 105 Fuzhou Road on Christmas morning was the largest disaster seen by the fire brigade in recent years in terms of surrounding property. The amount of water required for a single dousing reached 1.5 million gallons. (Relocation of the Office) After the fire brigade's main office moved from the Police Department to the Central Police Station building this year, it moved from the original rented house at the corner of Henan Road and Hankou Road to the original site of the Police Department's Traffic Section. (Ambulance Team Affairs) The ambulance team concurrently run by the Fire Department was dispatched a total of 7,239 times this year, of which 5,145 times were for accidental emergency medical conditions, and the rest were for hospitals to use ambulances to transport patients to and from. This is the fifth year that the team has been under the management of the Fire Department. In view of the team's effective work, reducing the pain of accidental injuries and illnesses, it is felt that the team's existence is an indispensable part of the municipality. Furthermore, this year an ambulance was stationed permanently at the Huishan Fire Station. The vehicle was dispatched a total of 409 times. Recently, in view of the increasing prosperity of industry in the eastern district, it is planned to dispatch an ambulance permanently to the Zhoujiazui Fire Station this year. In addition, it is planned to add a motorcycle for use when other vehicles are being repaired. (Traffic Congestion Problem) The most difficult thing for the fire brigade to do when dispatched at present is the traffic congestion on the road, making it difficult to reach the scene of the incident in the shortest possible time. Fortunately, the traffic police avoid and rarely deliberately obstruct the situation. Although there have been many accidents involving fire engines on duty, fortunately the losses are still minor. Only once did a fire engine No. 18 of Yangshupu drive from its station to the scene of the incident and reach the corner of Dalianwan Road and Huade Road, where a cyclist disregarded the police officer's command. The driver wanted to avoid him, causing him to crash into a store on the side of the road. Two firefighters were injured, and the cyclist and a pedestrian were seriously injured and died. (Cases of Arson) In terms of cases of arson, the number of incidents this year has decreased compared to the average number in previous years. There was only one final judgment this year, that is, the owner and accountant of a fabric shop quarreled and set fire to the shop on October 19. Later, the court sentenced the shop owner to three years and six months in prison and the accountant to ten months in prison.

A Visit to Guanshengyuan Farm 165

— Qian Hua

The three characters "Guanshengyuan" are deeply imprinted in the hearts of the general public. Especially children, who hope their parents will bring back sweets and biscuits produced by Guanshengyuan. When three or four friends are looking for an elegant and delicious place for snacks, they also shout the slogan "Let's go to Guanshengyuan." The success of Guanshengyuan is a story of struggle by its founder, Mr. Xian Guansheng. From a small food stall with a few hundred dollars, it has expanded into a large company with a capital of 500,000 yuan. Now, it has 14 branches and sub-branches across the country, two factories, and one farm and one plum orchard in Meilin. It employs thousands of people, which is truly no easy feat.

Last winter, on December 22nd, this reporter visited the Guanshengyuan Farm in Caohejing with the curator Yi. The facilities and layout were quite satisfactory. The person leading the tour recounted the founding and current status of Guanshengyuan, saying, "The founder of Guanshengyuan, Mr. Xian Guansheng, is from Nanhai, Guangdong, and came from a very humble background. At the age of sixteen, he apprenticed at a food store on Wuma Road. After completing his apprenticeship, he scraped together some small capital and opened a small food store called 'Guanxiang' on the left side of the Hunan New Stage in Shanghai. Later, when the New Stage moved to Mudan Road, Guanxiang also closed down due to sluggish business. Four years later, he opened a Tao Tao Ju food store at the original site of Wing On Company on Nanjing Road. In less than a year, due to the need to demolish and rebuild the building, he had to announce its closure again. In 1918, he and old friends from the opera world, Xia Yueshan and Zheng Zhengqiu, pooled a few hundred dollars to establish Guanshengyuan. They changed their business strategy, promoted profit-making for street vendors, and business boomed. Initially, the products were limited to preserved tangerine peel, fruit juice jelly, beef jerky, and a few other items. The following year, they built their own factory on Xiejiao Jumen Road, established a branch in Hankou, and the number of products increased daily, and sales expanded. In 1923, the capital was increased to 100,000 yuan, and it was reorganized as a limited company. In 1927, the capital was increased by another 50,000 yuan, and the total annual sales exceeded one million yuan. In 1931, the capital was increased by another 150,000 yuan, bringing the total to 300,000 yuan. In 1932, they began planning for the self-sufficiency of food raw materials, established a farm in Caohejing, and added a plum orchard in Chaoshan, Zhejiang. In 1934, the capital was increased by another 200,000 yuan, bringing the total to 500,000 yuan. That year, the total sales reached over 2.7 million yuan. Despite the economic downturn last year, there was still considerable progress in business."

The Caohejing farm that this reporter visited covers an area of ​​more than 40 mu, planted with many vegetables and fruits, to supply the restaurants of Guanshengyuan stores with ingredients for dishes. In the vacant spaces, pavilions were built, ponds were dug to draw in springs, and rocks were piled up to form mountains. A restaurant is located in the center of the farm, specially for those who come to the suburbs to breathe in the fresh air of nature and immerse themselves in the beautiful scenery, which invigorates the spirit and brings indescribable joy. Because it was winter, although it was a Sunday, there were only a few of us as visitors, and the quietness and desolation made it even more elegant and pleasant. A small part of the farm is designated as a goldfish garden, surrounded by bamboo fences. At the entrance, there is a horizontal plaque with the three characters "Fish Swim Heaven". Inside, there are ponds and fish tanks, holding thousands of goldfish of various sizes and colors. The rare and precious varieties are richly collected, reminiscent of visiting the Central Park and Tianqiao Goldfish Garden in Beiping, which is truly worth appreciating. The weather in the south is warmer, and in winter, the fish tanks can be exposed to sunlight without having to be moved indoors, saving a lot of trouble.

In the western part of the farm, there is a four-story building, which is the Guanshengyuan Caohejing Candy and Biscuit Factory. It occupies 60 square feet and is entirely built of cement and steel, with a three-dimensional shape and a magnificent appearance. Inside, the front of the first floor is the office, and the back is the boiler room. The second floor is the biscuit manufacturing department, the third floor is the packaging department, and the fourth floor is the candy department. All are powered by electricity, making it a modern factory. Male and female employees in each department were busy working, all wearing white cloth uniforms and white hats, clean and hygienic. The biscuit manufacturing department has several of the latest American-style baking ovens, each of which can produce more than 1,000 pounds of biscuits per hour. In addition, there are more than a dozen of the latest biscuit stamping machines, which can be used to make sweet, savory, and sandwich biscuits. The main parts of the machines are imported from Europe, and the auxiliary parts are made in Shanghai. After visiting each department, we rested in Wangmei Pavilion. The tea server brought strong tea, and everyone tasted the various freshly made biscuits, discussing the future development plans of the farm. Outside the window, we saw several plum trees with old trunks and graceful branches, their sparse shadows slanting across, making us feel relaxed and happy. After thanking the leader, our group reluctantly got into the car and returned.

Shanghai Basketball Association: Haizhe narrowly defeats Zhenru 168

42 to 41 – a one-point difference

Datong defeats Dahuajia YIA: Dahua forfeits

Youyou defeats Zhendan Yiyi: 50 to 23

Xie Xing to Battle Mailing Tonight 169

Zhenru versus Haizhe, yesterday's match at the China venue was part of the Shanghai Basketball Association's Jiajia group competition. Despite the heavy snowfall, the audience was still very enthusiastic. The fierce battle lasted for forty minutes. Zhenru led throughout the first half, but after the restart, Haizhe's momentum became overwhelming. This side defended, showing extremely fierce competition and excellent performance, making it one of the most exciting scenes in the league. In the end, Haizhe narrowly escaped with a 42-41 victory. The battle situation is as follows:

Zhenru scores the first five points. When lining up for the jump ball, Haizhe's dangerous player, Lan Yin, was not on the court, and Bai Naite temporarily took his place. Before a single round, Kuang Yao Ya caught a pass from Cai Binxiong under the basket and scored. Afterwards, Han and Cai attacked from the front and rear, both scoring twice. In an instant, it was 10-0, briefly shining brightly.

Haizhe scores one point. The Haizhe team only scored one point with a free throw by Peer. Seeing the unfavorable situation, Lan Yin was brought in as a fresh force, and Bai Naite retired. Under the sharp offensive of Zhenru, there was still not much development. Yin, Han, Kuang, and Wang assisted, adding to the score. On the other side, Lan Yin also managed to score several times. By the end of the break, Zhenru was far ahead at 21-12.

Lan Yin achieves his wishes. Changing the defensive zone, the dispute started again. Haizhe greatly demonstrated its usual techniques of robbery and looting. In addition, the tall Lan Yin's jump balls went exactly where he wanted. No matter how capable our players were, they were no match for him. As a result, the forwards gained a great advantage. In an instant, Shi, Lan, and Peer scored seven goals by attacking from different directions, and the score rose to 26-21, taking the lead in one fell swoop.

Both sides achieve a tie. Amidst the many difficulties, Zhenru changed its strategy and tried to counterattack. Wang Yong and Han scored three points with three shots, and the situation gradually turned around. Cai Yanxiong made a special achievement in the chaos, and then scored a long shot, creating a tie at 30.

Suffering a defeat by one point. Helplessly, the Haizhe team launched a comeback again. Shi, Lan, and Peer attacked from three directions, and Kalsen and Shi Guia intercepted from the front and rear. Zhenru's home was once again in turmoil. Then, Yin Guiren made a surprise attack, Nan Zhen lifted the moon under the basket, and Cai Yanxiong made three arrows from Tianshan, bringing the score to 39-41. Just as things were turning around, Cai unfortunately lost an opportunity, and Kalsen scored a point in return. Fortunately, Wang Nanzhen quickly retaliated, making it 42-41. Unfortunately, time ran out, and they suffered a defeat by one point.

In the B1 group, Youyou defeats Zhendan.

At the beginning of the fierce battle between Youyou and Zhendan, Youyou's battle situation was extremely smooth, scoring eight points in one go. However, Zhendan was unyielding and tried to counterattack, also showing some strength, taking the lead at 10-8. Afterwards, Youyou became even more courageous, and the score soared. Although Zhendan made repeated efforts, they were dwarfed by comparison. The result was 50-23, with Youyou winning.

Public Concession: This Year's Education Budget 178

Before the Financial Situation Recovers

Various Expenses Must Still Be Reduced

The 1936 budget of the Education Department of the Public Concession's工部局, which was previously discussed at two meetings by the Education Committee on January 21st and 28th, was recommended to the Board of Directors. Subsequently, it was approved by the Board of Directors and submitted to the Finance Committee for review. We will now disclose its outline and key points.

In terms of temporary education expenses, there are two houses planned to be added for Western children, one is the cooking and needlework room for the Western Girls' School on Yuyuan Road, and the other is the auditorium for the Western Elementary School, as well as other minor reconstructions. The former originally planned to build a two-story building. The Director of Finance strongly stated that the current financial situation is extremely difficult, and these buildings, including the auditorium of the elementary school, should be postponed. However, the Chairman of the Education Committee insisted that the cooking room should not be delayed any longer. As a result, a compromise was reached, and it was proposed to allocate 25,000 yuan for the construction of the cooking room as a Class A urgent expense. As for the elementary school auditorium, it will not be discussed for the time being. However, to facilitate students placing their bicycles, a shed should be built immediately, with a cost ranging from 300 to 400 yuan. This item has also been included in the Class A urgent items.

Recurring Expenses: Chinese School Section 179

As for the recurring expenses for the Chinese children's school section, the student-teacher ratio at the Huishan Road East District Elementary School is not high. The Director of Finance asked whether there was any possibility of reducing the number of teachers. The Director of the Education Department stated that the number of students at the school had increased from 405 to 425 since the last report from the Director of Finance, and that the number of places was limited due to the small size of the classrooms. As far as the current situation is concerned, there is no possibility of reducing the number of staff. The school's budget was immediately passed as originally proposed.

The number of students at the Huade Road Elementary School has increased. According to the original proposal of the Director of Finance, it was proposed to transfer one teacher from the East District Elementary School to the school. However, since it is not possible to reduce the number of staff at the East District Elementary School for the time being, it will be necessary to hire another teacher. The school's original budget and the estimate for hiring another teacher were all passed.

The newly established Chinese Children's Half-Day School on Wenjian师路 was originally planned to open seven classes and hire twelve teachers. The Director of Finance felt that the number of teachers was not needed so many. The Chairman of the Education Committee immediately stated that the school is open for six full days a week, with a total of 350 students, divided into two classes in the morning and evening, each attending classes for three hours. Therefore, it is feared that the twelve teachers are already feeling very tired at work. The Director of the Education Department stated that the school has not yet opened, and 318 students have been enrolled. This is still in the trial phase, and it is difficult to predict how many teachers will be needed in the future. However, they will do their best to economize in the future.

The above budget items, together with the recurring expenses of the Education Department and the recurring expenses of other elementary schools and night schools, have been passed and submitted to the Finance Committee for review.

Chinese Children's Middle School Budget Passed 180

The Singapore Road Girls' Middle School originally planned to hire four teachers this year, later changed to three, with one hired in January and two more hired in September in the autumn. However, the Finance Department strongly disagreed with this. A member of the Education Committee stated that the school has a definite income, so he believes that necessary expenses should not be withheld. The Chairman also said that since the number of students at the school has increased, it seems that there is no reason why teachers cannot be added. As a result, it was decided to add one teacher in the autumn, but it should be determined based on the situation at that time. After this case was revised, it was passed and recommended to the Board of Directors together with the recurring expenses budgets of other middle schools.

The工部局 established a normal school, which had previously been recommended to be discontinued by the Director of the Education Department. However, the school's expenses, totaling 2,900 yuan, were still included in the 1936 budget. Subsequently, the Chinese members of the Education Committee advocated using this expense to add a girls' night school in the East District. The Director of Finance stated that he did not oppose the proposal to add a girls' night school, but the expenses should not exceed the original 2,900 yuan for the normal school. As a result, it was decided to discontinue the normal school and use its expenses of 2,900 yuan to add a girls' night school.

Situation of Western Schools' Budgets 181

According to the original plan of the Western Elementary School, it was planned to hire one teacher in the spring and autumn seasons this year. Later, the principal of the school suggested that since the increase in the number of students in the spring season was not very large, only one teacher should be hired in the autumn. According to the Director of Finance, the teacher hired in the autumn was also not needed. The Director of the Education Department said that if the number of students increased sharply in the autumn, they would have to reject new students if they did not add teachers. As a result, it was decided that if the number of students increased in the autumn of this year, a first-grade teaching assistant should be hired from September 1st, and the expenses should be included in the budget in advance.

Furthermore, the Director of Finance expressed his dissatisfaction with the number of students in other Western schools in his report, saying that the current ratio of students to education units is only 21 students per unit. If this does not increase for a long time, the number of teachers should be reduced immediately, or no substitute teachers should be hired during the long vacations that teachers are entitled to. After deliberation by the Education Committee, it was decided that the Director of the Education Department should prepare a report on this matter and submit it to the committee for review.

The above education budgets, except for those that still need to be reviewed by the Finance Department, have been passed and submitted to the Finance Committee for review.

Children's Educational Novel: Little Men (One) (Seven) (Zero) 186

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Chapter Nine: Human Legacy of Love

"Wake up, Demi, dear! I want you to come."

"Oh, I just got to bed; it isn't daylight yet," said Demi, waking from his first sound sleep and blinking like a little owl.

"It's only ten o'clock, but your father is ill, and we must go to see him. Oh, my poor Joanie, my poor Paine," sighed Aunt Meg, bending over his pillow as she spoke. Demi, who was still sleepy, suddenly woke up, his heart filled with fear and surprise. He vaguely felt why Aunt Meg called him "Joanie" and cried for him, as if some misfortune had befallen him. He only clung to her, not saying a word. Soon she calmed down, saw his dejected face, gave him a loving kiss, and said:

"We must go and say good-bye to him, my dear, and without delay. So dress quickly, and come to my room."

"Yes, I will," Demi said. After Aunt Meg left, Demi quietly got up, dressed, still not knowing if he was awake or dreaming. Seeing Tommy still fast asleep, he didn't wake him. He just passed through the silent house, feeling that a sad and unprecedented thing was about to happen—this thing temporarily separated him from the other children, making the world seem dark, lonely, and strange, just like those rooms at night. Mr. Laurie's carriage was parked at the door. Little May was also ready in a moment. The brother and sister, guarded by their aunt and uncle, held hands all the way, sitting in the car, swiftly and silently passing through many shadowy roads, straight to the town to bid farewell to their father forever.

North-South Goods: Water Seals and Fluctuations in Bohai Date Prices 194

Due to the severe cold and thick ice at Dagukou, Tianjin, ships carrying red and black dates are unable to arrive, leading to a shortage of goods on the market. This has caused a sudden surge in prices. Red dates have increased by one yuan. For example, top-quality Southern-style red dates are now selling for sixteen yuan; first-grade red dates are selling for thirteen and a half to ten and a half yuan; second-grade red dates are selling for ten to nine and a half yuan; and standard red dates are selling for eight yuan. The market for black dates is even tighter, as the production and inventory are both limited. Only a few thousand packages remain in storage, causing vendors to hold tight to their goods and refrain from selling. Currently, Southern-style dates are being quoted two yuan higher than before. Top-grade Gaocheng dates are being offered at twenty yuan, second-grade Gaocheng dates at sixteen or seventeen yuan, Gaocheng standard dates at eleven yuan, and ordinary dates at nine and a half yuan. It is said that the local prices have also risen by about six jiao.

Piece Goods: Woolen Fabric Trading Favoring Japanese Products 195

The sales of woolen fabrics have been quite brisk recently. The purchasing power from various regions is strong. Merchants from Sichuan, Jiangxi, the capital, Changsha, and other ports are continuing to replenish their stocks, either by personally coming to Shanghai for procurement or by ordering through express mail. There are several such transactions daily, with Japanese goods being particularly favored. The reason is that buyers often find Western goods too expensive and the styles outdated. As a result, Japanese woolen fabrics now hold a considerable market share, and there is concern that Western woolen fabrics may be displaced. Yesterday, the sales of lightweight woolen fabrics and plain serge from various firms amounted to over six thousand yards. The transaction price for 160-count lightweight spring woolen fabric was three yuan and two jiao per yard, first-grade at three yuan and four and a half jiao, second-grade at two yuan and seven and a half jiao. The transaction price for 500-count ordinary gray plain serge was three yuan and four jiao, 1600-count at three yuan and four jiao, 1000-count at two yuan and seven and a half jiao, and 2500-count at two yuan and nine and a half jiao.

Galangal Shortage Leads to Price Increase of Two Yuan 196

Galangal, a type of spice, is also used medicinally. Recently, due to depleted inventory, prices have increased in both Shantou and Shanghai. It is said that most of the firms have already opened, with prices rising by one or two yuan. Future shipments are expected to be limited due to high production costs, making it difficult to meet the market demands.

Special Report: Draft Cotton Seed Law and Implementation Regulations 197

The China Cotton Improvement Association, noting that the United States, India, Egypt, and other countries have long had cotton seed laws, and that domestic cotton production has developed significantly in recent years, believes that it is essential to implement a cotton seed law to enhance and improve the effectiveness of cotton production. Therefore, at its third annual general meeting on December 28, 1934, it was decided to "draft a cotton seed law and implementation regulations and submit them to the central government for adoption and implementation." Wang Yao-chen, Feng Zhao-chuan, Feng Ze-fang, Hao Qin-ming, and Jiang Di-xian were elected as drafting committee members, with Hao Qin-ming leading the drafting process. Over the past year, based on the domestic cotton production situation and with reference to the laws of the United States, India, and Egypt, a draft cotton seed law consisting of twenty-four articles and implementation regulations consisting of thirteen articles have been prepared. These were then submitted to the fourth annual meeting on January 5, 1936, for discussion. It was generally agreed that these laws are unprecedented in China and that opinions should be solicited from all over the country to ensure their perfection. It was decided to publish the draft first and solicit opinions from all parties within three months. The drafting committee will then revise the draft based on the feedback, and the executive committee will decide whether to submit it to the central government. The draft cotton seed law and implementation regulations are recorded below. If you have any opinions, please send them to the China Cotton Improvement Association at No. 260, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai, before the end of April.

Draft Cotton Seed Law 198

(Article 1) In this law, "cotton seeds" refers to all cotton seeds used for planting (hereinafter referred to as "seeds for planting"). Those used for oil extraction, animal feed, fertilizer, etc., are not subject to this restriction. (Article 2) From the date of promulgation of this law, all existing cotton varieties shall be investigated and registered by the Central Cotton Improvement Institute and announced nationwide. New varieties bred or imported shall also be subject to review and registration by the Central Cotton Improvement Institute before they can be promoted. (Article 3) Applicants for variety registration must submit a detailed description of the results of years of testing, various characteristics, and the proposed promotion area, along with samples of plant fibers and seeds, to the Central Cotton Improvement Institute for review and registration. Those approved for promotion will be issued a registration certificate. (To be continued)
