Women's Special

Dedicated to the Newlywed Housewife 199

— He Gui

Ladies, time flies so quickly. Before you know it, you've left your original family and become the mistress of another. This new family is indeed the haven you've always dreamed of. However, as you embark on your journey as a new housewife, you're bound to encounter countless challenges. You wonder how to maintain lasting love with your husband and how to manage this newly established household. Even minor issues can bring you to tears. Perhaps you'll even start to resent the troubles and hardships of marriage!

Ladies, you must remember that your own mother went through similar difficulties when she first became a housewife. But she persevered and raised you and your siblings. She then passed on the responsibility of being a housewife, a duty that every woman must inevitably shoulder, to you. She is your best role model. You should strive to emulate her virtues. Naturally, she may have made mistakes along the way. Consider those missteps as valuable lessons and avoid repeating them in your own new family.

For instance, you may be concerned about how to maintain lasting love between husband and wife. This isn't as difficult as it seems. Aside from mutual tolerance and understanding, the most crucial factor is realizing that your love isn't built on material wealth. Your parents may have occasionally quarreled, and most of their disagreements likely stemmed from financial matters. Countless happy couples have suffered irreparable damage due to disputes over money. You must avoid making the same mistakes. If your husband's income is modest and he can't afford to dress you in finery or provide lavish meals, you might feel inadequate when you see classmates and friends with more material possessions. You might blame your husband for being incompetent, lament your fate, or even be tempted to be unfaithful to your husband to satisfy your material desires. On the other hand, if your husband is wealthy and provides you with a life of luxury, you might feel like you're in paradise. But indulging in endless wants and desires will ultimately bring you no benefit. Aren't those who live solely for material possessions considered "walking corpses?"

Think about the great women in history. Were they frugal or extravagant? As educated women, you surely know many examples. Yang Guifei and Empress Dowager Cixi have been dead for years, but people still criticize them. You also know the story of Liang Hong and Meng Guang, a couple who lived a simple life but were praised by later generations for their virtue.

So, you see, whether your husband is rich or poor, you must break free from the "demon" of material desires to maintain lasting love between you and your husband.

If these words have struck a nerve, then I hope you will quickly change your ways. Happiness can still be yours. Otherwise, you will face great suffering in this life. Regardless of your family's circumstances, both you and your husband must strive to move forward. Don't stagnate for the sake of momentary comfort. You should also constantly encourage your husband to advance, and your love will grow stronger each day, filling your new family with joy and happiness.

The Only Female Astronomer in the Far East 200

— Xi Qian

——Mrs. Zou Yixin of China——

In our country, which lags behind in every aspect, various sciences naturally fall behind those of other nations. Japan, as a rising nation, is always competing with European and American countries in everything. However, it has yet to produce a female astronomer, leaving Mrs. Zou Yixin of China to excel in this field and bring honor to China's new women. The following is a brief account of the Japanese people's praise for Ms. Zou, for the benefit of our readers.

This year, the Japanese astronomical community is welcoming a distinguished guest from China because of the numerous opportunities to observe solar eclipses. She is Zou Yixin, a technician at the National Central University Observatory in Nanjing. There are no aspiring female astronomers in Japan, so Mrs. Zou will be the only female astronomer in the Orient. She received her education at Central University and then became a technician at her alma mater's observatory, where she frequently publishes papers. Because China's astronomical observation equipment is not complete, she came to Japan for further study. Through the mediation of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Education, she will be a guest at the Tokyo Astronomical Observatory in Mitaka Village, Tokyo Prefecture, starting in mid-March of this year. There are five or six Chinese students studying astronomy in Japan, but only Mr. Shen and Mr. Xu have graduated from the astronomy department. Mr. Shen and others have gone to Germany and have earned considerable reputation. These are all men and they studied in Japan. Now, Mrs. Zou has come to Japan for practical training after studying astronomy in her own country, which is even more valuable. Mrs. Zou is the first female astronomer in the Orient.

How pitiful are those women who only know how to apply rouge and powder to their faces, but don't understand the prices of firewood, rice, oil, and salt!

—Special Feature of this Newspaper

Mrs. Tai Shuangqiu, Ms. Huang Jima, Discusses Home Economics Education 201

— Ji Ping

Home economics education is such an important subject, especially in this era of prevalent modern family systems. Encouraged by this thought, I made a special trip to visit Ms. Huang Jima, who is not only a pioneer in social service but also a virtuous wife and mother of the new era. Dr. Tai used to teach at various universities in Guangdong and Henan, and she accompanied him to serve there as well. Later, when he became the dean of the College of Education at Great China University, she also served as a lecturer at Great China. She also provided a lot of assistance to his founding of the "Educational Compilation and Translation Bureau," his launch of the "Twenty-Two Society Movement," and his invention of the "Shuangqiu Alphabet and Educational Vehicle." Wouldn't you say that such a capable wife is worth emulating by women in general? The following is a fragmented record of our conversation at the time:

The Motivation for Studying Medicine

Mrs. Tai said: "Mr. Tai and I were classmates at National Southeast University. He was a year ahead of me. I studied foreign literature, and he studied education. Later, when he went to study in the United States, I felt that foreign languages were not practical, so I transferred to Peking Union Medical College, thinking that I could become a doctor if I advanced, or guide general family health issues if I retreated. However, my constitution was too weak, and I couldn't endure the hard work, so I returned to Southeast University to graduate. When I arrived in Shanghai, I suddenly wanted to continue studying medicine. Coincidentally, West Gate had just founded a women's medical university, so I studied for another two years, completed the required credits, and had a basic understanding of medicine. At this time, Mr. Tai returned to China and did not approve of my pursuit of medicine. He wanted me to serve education alongside him. In fact, learning specialized skills can also contribute to education. This is what I like, and I don't want to violate my own aspirations."

The Contribution of Home Economics Education

After we formed our family, we implemented our predetermined plan and devoted ourselves to education. Three years ago, when we were at Henan University, the provincial women's normal school hired me to teach home economics. I felt that the women in the Northwest were very simple, hardworking, and tolerant. The original home economics course only taught common sense such as cooking and sewing, which was certainly not enough. So, I decided to expand the scope and compile my own lecture notes, focusing on: Family health—such as physical protection, health checkups, prevention of infectious diseases, first aid and nursing for common illnesses, and home medicine equipment; Women's childbirth—such as prenatal and postnatal hygiene, infant care, the development of infants' living habits, and the handling of illnesses; Family education—such as child psychology, children's behavior, and guidance in intellectual, moral, and physical aspects; Family economy—such as budgeting and final accounting, savings and insurance, and household bookkeeping; Family social activities... I explained these essential knowledge for women in detail, classified by categories. The students were very interested and tasted them. After teaching for a year and a half, I asked them if they had learned these theories before. Everyone said no. I said that all of you will be housewives in the future, so this kind of knowledge must be applied in practice. I think that a woman who does not understand home economics is not worthy of being a housewife; let alone building a new family and reforming a corrupt society. Just talking about serving the society is also very vague. Returning to Shanghai in recent years, I have been serving in the home economics department at Daxia University, reorganizing the previous purchases and publishing two books: one is "Practical Home Economics" and the other is "Home Affairs", wanting to instill home economics into forward-thinking women.

My Opinion on Women's Service

I believe that modern women who only stay at home as housewives cannot give full play to their abilities and do social undertakings that are beneficial to the public. It is too narrow. On the other hand, only serving the society and despising home affairs is not the happiness of the family. In fact, there should be no obvious distinction between family service and social service. These two aspects should be integrated, because social service can be said to be indirectly serving other people's families, while family service is directly serving one's own family. So, I advocate that a woman should recognize that in family service, she should also engage in social service undertakings. Nowadays, some urban women do not go out, and some spend their days in recreation, and there are very few proper contacts between women. I want to organize a club that meets once a week for a decision, has proper entertainment, and has public lectures where knowledge can be exchanged and issues of interest to oneself can be studied. No matter what kind of knowledge, if one person understands it, the benefits are limited, but if the public knows it, the results will be huge; if you want every family to be happy, you can't do without this kind of common gathering.

The Tai Family

Their family is also worth emulating. Mr. Tai is almost out serving all day long, and Mrs. Tai presides over the household affairs. They have no improper habits such as smoking, drinking, or gambling, and devote themselves to books, newspapers, writings, and sports. It is said that the household expenses are more economical than ordinary middle-class families. Babies in other families eat milk, chicken juice, and tonics, while their children only drink soy milk and rice soup. This is the idea of Mr. and Mrs. Tai. From this point alone, you can get a general idea of the rest. Mr. Tai's diligent and thrifty spirit is equal to that of an old farmer in the countryside. He wears cotton clothes all over his body, and each piece of clothing costs no more than three or four yuan. This leader of the frugal movement can indeed speak and act, unlike ordinary people who love to be leaders, with mouths full of benevolence, righteousness, and morality, but their hearts are not worth mentioning. I saw the couplet written by Mr. Han Guojun in the hall of the department:

Ten thousand volumes in the chest can support the hungry world, not a speck of dust reaches the door.

After careful reflection, I felt that it was most appropriate to describe the character of Mr. and Mrs. Tai with this couplet.

(Mrs. Tai and Her Beloved Daughter) 202

Japanese Female Writers in the Past Year (Japan Communication) 203

— Man Zhi

Generally speaking, the status of Japanese women in society is very low, but they have a high level of performance in literature. Summing up the works published in various magazines in the past year, whether in terms of quantity or quality, there are considerable achievements.

How many female writers have expressed their works in the past year? According to the customary division, they can be roughly divided into two major schools: bourgeois literature and proletarian literature. The authors of bourgeois literature include Nogami Yaeko, Uno Chiyo, Hayashi Fumiko, Okada Teiko, Enchi Fumiko, Mikawa Yoko, Nakamachi Teiko, Tomimoto Yoko, Yada Tsuseko, etc. Proletarian writers include Nakajo Yuriko, Hirabayashi Taiko, Kubokawa Ineko, Hirabayashi Hideko, Matsuda Tokiko, Otani Fujiko, and new writer Asai Hanako, etc. However, even among bourgeois writers, works such as Nogami Yaeko's "Poor Boy" cannot be classified in the same category as Uno Chiyo and Hayashi Fumiko's works. "Poor Boy" is full of positive liberal ideas and expresses extreme resistance to modern Japanese society. Okada Teiko, Enchi Fumiko, Tomimoto Yoko, and others' works also strongly carry this color, which is rarely seen in the works of bourgeois male writers. It can be said that Japanese female writers' liberalism preserves its purity more than male writers.

In addition to "Poor Boy," Nogami Yaeko also wrote "Little Devil's Song," which was based on the riots at Hosei University and used her husband as one of the central figures in the novel. Many criticisms have said that her observation of the people around her is not thorough. "Poor Boy" describes a young boy's heart being hurt by military training. It is an enlightenment work.

Uno Chiyo's "Eroticism," "Me and the Child," "Joy of Separation," "Women's Lives," "Prostitute's Letter," etc., mostly depict the erotic world.

Hayashi Fumiko wrote "Foggy Days," "Clara," "Life Rhapsody," "Hen," "Grape Bank," "Oyster," etc. In "Oyster" and "Foggy Days," it can be seen that the author is trying to transition from lyricalism to observational literature, especially "Oyster," which has received good reviews from the literary world.

Okada Teiko wrote the drama "Miss Xu Xu Aisha," which satirizes the issue of a certain lady preparing to be betrothed to the Emperor of Abyssinia as a royal sword. Enchi Fumiko also published dramas, such as "Forgery Incident," etc.

Among the proletarian faction, Nakajo Yuriko is the most prominent. In the past year, she wrote "Breast" and "Breakwater," and then fell into a situation where she could not write. "Breakwater" was also written during her life as a prisoner. "Breast" has received very good reviews in many criticisms. Mitsuharu Serizawa said that it is a good work that combines daily life and history.

Hirabayashi Taiko is the most prolific writer in the proletarian faction in the past year, writing "Sakura," "A Material on the Theory of the Intellectual Class," "Octopus," "Saturday Night," "Women's Problems," etc. "Sakura" is a satirical work. "A Material on the Theory of the Intellectual Class" is a typical work that critically depicts the intellectual class because of the lively discussions about the intellectual class in the Japanese forum in the past year. "Octopus" is a work depicting unstable figures in the laboring class. What is particularly noteworthy is "Women's Problems," which is a work that raises questions from the perspective of women about the liberal views of men and women who take women's economic independence and gender equality as their motto. In general, her works in the past year have been mainly social criticism.

Kubokawa Ineko wrote "A Bag of Coarse Snacks," "Among the Iron Filings," "Along the Way," etc. "A Bag of Coarse Snacks" is praised for being full of female psychology. "Along the Way" is a female worker's recollection of her girlhood. Matsuda Tokiko serialized the long novel "Villager" in "Women's Literature and Art."

Hirabayashi Hideko's "A Typical Example" and "Daily Affairs" are all based on her own personal experiences. Fujishima Maki published the long novel "In Insult" in "Literary Criticism." New writer Asai Hanako also wrote "Muddy Spring." Otani Fujiko published "Susakiya," "Mother's Letter," and "Blood Relationship," etc. In addition, new writers and their works include Uchiyama Ikuko's "Assistant" and Togawa Shizuko's Death and Life.

From the above description, it can be seen that Japanese female writers are active. But looking at our China, the literary activities of women in the past year have completely declined. Not only have no new female writers appeared, but even the established female writers have not developed, and there are no women engaged in literature. In this state, how should we strive to express women's creativity in literature!

Two Major Camps on Women's Issues 204

— Liu Yazi

Regarding women's issues, there are recently two major camps. On the one hand, it is said that men are human beings, and women are also human beings, so men and women should not be distinguished by gender, and should strive for the entire human race with the qualifications of human beings. On the other hand, they want to call women back to the kitchen and into the home, making cakes and puddings, and holding children, which is considered to be their natural duty, and is beautifully named the theory of virtuous mothers and good wives, or the new theory of virtuous mothers and good wives. Between these two, I agree with the former proposition. Virtuous mothers and good wives certainly sound good. Who would advocate that women should be unvirtuous mothers and wives? However, in the same proportion, men should be virtuous fathers and good husbands, which is always the great righteousness that cannot be escaped between heaven and earth. However, why not advocate virtuous fathers and good husbands? However, men have responsibilities beyond fathers and husbands; then, don't women have responsibilities beyond mothers and wives? My proposition is that in the future Datong world, there will be free love and public childcare, and even the names of parents, wives, and children will be gone, and of course there will be no virtuousness. In the present, the duties of fathers and husbands should be opposed to those of mothers and wives. Since no one has been heard to advocate virtuous fathers and good husbands, advocating virtuous mothers and good wives is always superfluous.

The tone of "Women's Life" belongs to the former. It can get rid of the clichéd virtuous mother and good wife, and advocates that women should strive for the entire nation, and even more for the entire human race. This proposition, I think, is worth supporting and worth introducing.

Editor's Note: This magazine has no preconceptions about women's issues, whether it is to enter society or the kitchen; we welcome articles on both sides of this debate.

Reproductive Maturity 206

— Yao Erchang

Reproductive maturity (Gesschechtsreife) refers to the completion of general reproductive organs and the ability to perform complete reproductive functions, which usually occurs during the onset of puberty. At this stage, men grow beards and their voices deepen, their muscles and bones become stronger. In women, their breasts become fuller, menstruation begins, their pelvises widen, and their skin becomes richer in sebum, forming the physique unique to women. If their reproductive glands are weak, men will suffer from premature ejaculation, impotence, spermatorrhea, and other symptoms. Women will suffer from amenorrhea, irregular periods, uterine cold, leucorrhea, and other symptoms. Each must be treated with endocrine preparations for male and female reproductive glands to restore their reproductive function. If the body is weak, it is not suitable for marriage. Even after marriage, there is no hope of offspring. It is for this reason that some people have been married for a long time and suffer from infertility.

Comments

The Movement to Liberate婢女 219

— Jianping

This newspaper listed on the 5th: the local Public Security Bureau decided to implement registration starting in March, stating that "liberating homeless女子 who are alone and helpless is extremely related to international reputation and humanitarian laws," and allow for "unconditional release" of婢女 to "restore freedom." This news can be considered worthy of a raised voice. Although in principle, it is only superficially for the sake of "international reputation," for the sake of "humanitarian laws," and not caring about the "homeless女子" being abused, but seeking a way out, the decisive disposal of their methods is also a commendable merit.

Now, what needs to be specially brought up for discussion are items 2, 3, and 4 in the "registration method" regarding the way out for婢女 after liberation.

Article 2 states: "If they are minors and have no home to return to, or if they return home but cannot afford to support themselves, they should be sent to the municipal welfare home or other charitable organizations for placement." This is almost the same meaning as item 4, "婢女 who have been liberated but have no family members or the location of family members is unknown may select the head of a local welfare home or other charitable organization as their guardian." It is very clearly "humanitarian" to unconditionally pity and "guard" the婢女. In principle, this can be said to be appropriate, but we can say that it is not thorough. Because the true freedom that a person needs is to have true skills to support themselves, not to need anyone to rely on. Although perhaps the welfare home has ways to teach the婢女 skills, the way out for the welfare home is nothing more than "public selection of a match," isn't that again "impossible"? Therefore, we hope that "婢女 who have been liberated" need a strict training institution to enable them to learn a skill by themselves; and there is a need for an employment agency to guide their career paths. That is true liberation, that is true freedom. As for item 3, for those who are adults (over sixteen years old), "seek their consent and choose a match for them." This is also a mistake caused by not understanding the principle that "a woman's way out is not to rely on her husband after marriage" as mentioned above. From these three incomplete methods, I am reminded that the reason for their liberation is fundamentally incomplete. They should take "婢女's true way out, true freedom as a major premise, and then they can study the thorough method.

Untitled 220

— Chenji

It is difficult for me to settle on a "title," I am very sad

A "primary school teacher" is a symbol of sadness right now. I am a "primary school teacher."

School has started. How difficult is my heart! —— The most difficult thing is: I can't even tell myself whether I am happy or sad?

I ran into the classroom with such a mood. Because the "timetable" has not yet been arranged, I talk to the children about current affairs or some principles of "how to be a person".

I am speaking so enthusiastically. I saw that the facial expressions of each child were tense or relaxed following the tension of my speech. However, what surprised me was an exceptionally new child whose face had no expression, only two eyebrows were standing on his eyes so melancholically, he neither smiled nor was indignant; his face was a pool of stagnant water!

When I stopped speaking, I remembered: Not many days ago, the school arranged for me to be on duty at the school. It was during the winter vacation, and all my colleagues had gone out, leaving me alone in the school. An elderly man came in and asked me, "Can I still register?" "Yes!" I replied. So he filled out the "registration form".

I asked him, "Is that child your son?"

"No! No!" He shook his head hurriedly, "He's my grandson!"

"He's your grandson?" I looked at his face. Saying he was an old man, he would not be over sixty. Yet he had a thirteen-year-old grandson.

He felt very uneasy about my suspicion. He coughed and immediately took out a handkerchief to cover his mouth. I saw tears floating in his eyes. I was surprised, "Why are there tears?" He pretended to blow his nose but I saw him wiping away the tears.

He sighed so lightly, fearing that others would know it was a sigh, and said, "Sir! That child studied in a private school in the countryside, or maybe his level in Shanghai is not enough, so I ask you, sir, to pay special attention!"

"Of course! Of course!" I saw him looking at me with such earnest eyes! After a while, he said:

"I'll pay the tuition and miscellaneous fees…"

He reached into his pocket and took out a handful of money. I gave him a receipt. He took the receipt and hurried away. I sent him to the door.

"Goodbye, sir!" His tone was slightly trembling.

"Goodbye! Goodbye!" His back was followed by a pile of sad ashes. …

Thinking of this, I looked very carefully at the face of the new child. —— It's a stagnant water face!

"Yes!" Very light, very light.

"Where does your dad do business?"

He just shook his head. I still thought he didn't understand my question, so I asked him again, speaking very slowly and clearly.

"Where does your dad do business?"

He shook his head and said, "No! No!"

"No business, unemployed?"

He seemed very embarrassed to answer me, but he had to answer me. He said, "No, my dad is dead!"

"Dead?"

Nodding.

"How many years has he been dead?"

"Six years."

"Then what about your mother?"

"She's dead too!"

He cried "wow". My heart was struck by a sharp sword. Some of the other children were staring at him in a daze, while others were saying with mocking faces

"Hey! He's crying! He's crying!"

The bell rang for the end of class. I didn't even have the courage to look at him. I quickly escaped into the "teachers' office." I regretted it so much. Why did I have to hurt this innocent little heart!

Alas! No son's sorrow, no mother's sorrow, alas! My tears also flowed down.

Night 221

— Hei Ding

Wang Lin had been sick for over ten days. Since the day he was driven out of the arsenal by soldiers on September 18th and lost his job, he had been spending his lonely days in distress. He walked the path of despair, in sorrow, in deep pain! He was like being trapped in a dark circle. He couldn't catch a comfortable breath. Like others, he had lost the guarantee of survival. He dared not think about this melancholic country, this vast and boundless field of sinful slaughter. He was truly worried that his family of four would be on the brink of starvation.

He had a wife and two children. The elder child was fourteen years old, named Xiao Mao. The younger child was not even three months old. Their lives were in an unspeakable state. He was bedridden, unable to get out of bed, due to his illness. Except for Xiao Mao and his mother, who secretly ran to the fields of the villagers in the eastern suburbs every day, carrying a large bamboo basket, to glean some corn, sorghum ears, and soybean pods to cook for the whole family to eat their fill, there was no other way to go.

However, winter was approaching soon. The lush and verdant countryside had become a desolate scene of withered yellow. From then on, they would not even have the blessing of eating corn, sorghum ears, and soybean pods.

They were treading a black line of starvation.

On the day before the New Year, Xiao Mao listened to his mother and went to his uncle's house in Huanggu Tun early in the morning, carrying a rice bag, intending to borrow some rice from his uncle to prepare for the New Year's meal tomorrow. Who knew that he would return home with disappointment: he said that his uncle's house only had a few bowls of rice left, and even he himself wouldn't have enough for tomorrow. Xiao Mao's mother sighed and looked at Xiao Mao's father, who was somewhat dazed at this moment. He closed his eyes and mumbled a few words in his throat, the last of which was: "Alas... just wait for death."

Evening. It was snowing. The northwest wind howled straight. Xiao Mao was not at home. He had gone out since noon and had not returned until now. Xiao Mao's mother and father suspected that he had gone to the residence of the Zhao family in Bianmen again to beg for leftovers. The little child refused to sleep and kept crying. There was no light in the room, and the surroundings were already a bit dim. The scraps of paper on the ceiling rustled non-stop. Xiao Mao's mother held the child, leaning against the wall. Xiao Mao's father lay beside Xiao Mao's mother, as if he was cold. He curled up tightly in a thin quilt. They didn't talk much. They hadn't eaten yet. They hoped that Xiao Mao would bring back the leftovers from that residence, they believed that Xiao Mao would do that. Their lives now depended on Xiao Mao alone: in the autumn, Xiao Mao went to the suburbs to glean corn, sorghum ears, and soybean pods, but in the winter, Xiao Mao had to go to people's doors every day to beg for leftovers to bring home. So they liked Xiao Mao very much.

The room was lonely. Adorned in this lonely air, it was truly a picture without the slightest pleasing color.

Just then, an alarming sound flew from the end of the alley, it seemed to be the sound of someone running, both chaotic and urgent. They were immediately frightened, wondering what trouble was brewing outside again! They listened carefully, but they couldn't hear people shouting, nor could they hear the gunshots that should have been there during a disturbance.

The sound came closer step by step, and went straight into the alley, and when the sound approached their gate, they only heard the gate being kicked open with a snap. Then a black shadow jumped into the room, and before they could see who it was, the person who jumped in shouted hoarsely and stutteringly: "Dad, Dad, Dad..."

Taking a breath, he continued, "Dad, quickly give me a sack..."

This shout was originally Xiao Mao. His appearance made them all afraid, so everyone's face had a kind of nervous flush.

Xiao Mao's father, in a daze, got up from the bed, jumped to the ground, grabbed Xiao Mao's wrist, trembling, and said: "You, you, what happened?"

Xiao Mao used a very dirty palm, grabbing haphazardly on his forehead several times: his palms were covered with sweat. He spat out a mouthful of spit, then cracked his lips: "This time, we are going to... you don't know, the Hengxingde Grain and Rice Store on 　　Street was robbed! There are so many people at the door, all holding rice bags. There was an argument in the room. I want to take the sack to grab some so we can celebrate the New Year tomorrow..."

Before Xiao Mao finished speaking, Xiao Mao's father jumped up almost crazily, he clenched his fist and said hatefully; "Go, I'll go too, otherwise we will starve to death..."

Xiao Mao's mother, hurriedly stepped forward and grabbed the lapel of Xiao Mao's father, and said in a pleading tone; "Xiao Mao's father, you are sick, you can't go, you are sick..."

But, he finally ran out the door, Xiao Mao followed behind. When they left the alley, Xiao Mao's mother stood blankly on the stone steps of the gate, raising her voice, shouting like this: "Xiao Mao, you must take good care of your father, don't be careless, life is important..."

However, they pretended not to hear, but ran like the wind towards 　　Street. Arriving at 　　Street, arriving at the entrance of Hengxingde, they squeezed into the crowd desperately. Xiao Mao couldn't squeeze in, at first he firmly held his father's clothes with his hand, but holding, hitting

Page 18

hitting, Xiao Mao was finally squeezed away, he looked up for a long time and finally he found his father carrying two bags of foreign flour out. But, at this moment, gunshots suddenly rang out outside the door. As a result, the large crowd gathered at the door ran away, fell down, and for a while, a tragic scene was presented. Under this condition, Xiao Mao's father loosened the two bags of foreign flour on his shoulders and quickly lay on the ground. Xiao Mao cried and shouted, and crawled on the ground with both hands. The gunshots tightened. After a while, Xiao Mao quietly curled up in the flowing pool of blood.

Night shrouded the earth. Four troop-carrying trucks of the ×× military garrison team flew from the main street in Bianmen.

Wagon Sheet Draped 222

— Especially

— Bitter Snow of Homecoming IV

These days, the entire mood is buried in joy, how can we express it? There is an indescribable emotion in the bottom of my heart!

The sky pulled down a sad face, cried tears, and piled lightly on the ground. Where did the gust of evil wind come from? It rolled up the accumulated tears and slammed wildly on every pedestrian and building. The shop signs rattled and squeaked.

We are running along the crisscrossing railroad tracks, stepping on the thick snow. It is estimated that the snow should be more than five inches! The heavy oil boots shattered the mirror-like snow surface. When you are not paying attention, if your foot steps on a bumpy place, it will jump into the shoe socket, and the coolness will penetrate from the soles of your feet to your dantian, and your body will shiver.

——Can you spot the wagon sheet? Xiao Wei asked me, holding a bag of things in his hand.

Wagon sheet? This is a new name in my ears.

——Don’t understand? He smiled, a sudden thought made him realize that this name was unfamiliar to me, so he greeted me and asked me to do the same work as him.

The south end and the north end have been almost everywhere, but the numbers on the wagon sheets are difficult to find. The ribbon on Xiao Wei's fur hat fluttered in the wind. The ears seemed to have been bitten off by a cat. The vast railway network was devoid of pedestrians.

Later, Xiao Wei really became anxious and didn't care about the cold wind. He took off his hat, grabbed his hair, and thought. Steam was billowing from the top of his head, and there was a solemn expression on his forehead that was not easy to see.

——Let’s do this, he decided, handing me part of the things in his hand: you go to that end to find it, and I will go somewhere else. We need to divide and cooperate. After a pause, he looked at the watch in his hand: Okay, hurry up, they are still waiting for us to go back for dinner!

Along the junction, I was calculating in my heart that there were still six wagon sheets missing. How can I find them? Really, I was a little scared. I thought, if I can’t find the wagon sheets as desired, maybe I will be subject to some unsatisfactory punishment? Fear was lurking in my throat.

Suddenly, there was a sound of hurried footsteps behind me. I looked at it and Xiao Wei ran over in a panic and said——

——Forgot, forgot, we will all be waiting for you at the street corner of the station for a while to gather there! After saying that, he left quickly against the wind and snow.

December, the day is very short, the street corner on that side has already lit up the street lights, dim, quickly swept down, everything only exists in a vague outline.

Let’s go back. I found three sections, and maybe the remaining ones were discovered among them, I thought like this. Following the dim street lights, I walked to the street corner that had been agreed upon!

——Why are you so late? We have been waiting for a long time. A Liu smiled: Let’s go, let’s go to 　　to fill our stomachs first. He pulled me and turned into the street corner.

In the hotel, we didn’t want to sleep. We were planning the only tomorrow. Who would buy what? How would we install the head car? And the food for the road, as well as what drinks and so on...

——We have to get up early tomorrow, go to bed.

——Tell the waiter not to let the charcoal fire go out.

Lying in the quilt, my heart will not be calm. The fire supports the warmth in the room. On the window, the zither is still playing a solo!

Special Feature

Notes on Visiting the Chiba Soy Sauce Industry in Japan (VII) 223

— (Ye Xiyuan)

After visiting these soy sauce companies in Chiba, we deeply felt that even the soy sauce business must be large-scale. Japanese soy sauce companies have at least a capital of one to two million or even twenty to thirty million, because of mass production and rationalization, the production cost will inevitably be reduced, and the market will inevitably expand. When we first went, although we were not without ambition, considering the backwardness of our country's economy, how could we expect to reach the same level; moreover, the people of our country only know how to engage in speculation, but do not know how to strive for the development of the national economic production business? After returning, because of the relationship between China and Japan, it was not calm, and we could not realize our ideals. In a blink of an eye, it has been four or five years. Now, when I hold the pen to write this article, although the Northeast is no longer our country, the people of our country should be aware: in the future, I still hope that our previous ideals can be realized one day, then I will not write this article in vain.

Finally, I must thank Mr. Namiki Jutarō of Noda Soy Sauce Company, Mr. Mogi Saheiji, Mr. Yonezawa Yasushi of Yamataka Soy Sauce Company, and Mr. Shinogi Shigeru and Mr. Hamaguchi Rinzo of Hatako Soy Sauce Company. This is because of their hospitality and leadership that we did not make this trip to Chiba in vain. Although the time has passed for several years, I wish their businesses will progress day by day and their health will progress day by day. (The End)

New Song Introduction 224

Song of the Lake

One of the songs from the Xinhua Records' "Song of Everlasting Regret"

Sung by Wang Renmei and Mei Xi, composed by He Luting (1) Paddle, paddle, paddle,

The bow of the boat paddles up flying waves,

Paddle, paddle, paddle,

Paddle until the sun sets in the west,

The shadow of the pagoda is slanting again.

The flocks of returning geese,

Fly to the ends of the earth in rows;

The schools of fish at the bottom of the water,

Play happily in the secluded springs;

Only the sinful human world,

Is forever struggling and killing;

The ideal world,

Is it just an ideal after all?

The light of the waves ripples with human figures,

Ripples with the rosy clouds of the western sky;

The withered lotus whispers softly,

The scattered crows on the withered willow.

Sing, sing;

Only on this quiet lake,

Can you sing to your heart's content;

Only when this lake is as picturesque,

Can there be a cloud of joy.

(2) Paddle, paddle, paddle,

The bow of the boat paddles up flying waves,

Paddle, paddle, paddle,

Paddle until the sun sets in the west,

The shadow of the pagoda is slanting again.

Illusions of couples on the lake;

The blood-red sunset in the western sky,

A cry of sorrow in the four fields;

Fallen leaves fall one after another.

I wish I could be a violent storm,

Roaring, roaring,

Destroying this human hell;

Cleansing this bloody world.

Temptation of the Radio Script of the Drama Troupe's Broadcasting Meeting (IV) 225

— (Screenplay by Liu Yawei)

Lao Wu: I don't believe it. I can't escape from anything that happens to me. No matter how great the difficulty, I will fight!

Big Brother: Lao Wu is right, so even if we die, we must die happily!

Xiao Lu: Lao Wu: You try to fight, but when you encounter death, who are you going to fight with?

A Qiao: Yes, death is fate. Do you want to slap God in the face twice?

Lao Wu: God? A joke! If God can't control us, is he worthy of controlling our death?

Xiao Lu: Then who are you going to fight with? Tell me quickly! Although I, Xiao Lu, am young, I am not weak. No matter what demon or ghost it is, if I punch it (hitting the table), at least it won't die, but it will be 80% dead!

Big Brother: I'm afraid you can't finish it by fighting? Old Wu　is right, what you said is indeed correct!

Big Brother: Xiao Lu, you shouldn't be confused. Do you know how the flood was caused?

Little Xiao Lu (seriously) I heard that the Yellow River breaches almost every year.

Big Brother: Whose responsibility is this?

Xiao Lu: I don't know!

Drama 228

Timely Society

Huaxing (1260 11:00 PM to 11:45 PM)

"Tragedy of the Lakeside"

A certain old man's daughter, named Bai Wei, also known as Su Ping, followed her father to study in Beiping in her childhood, and admired Yang Mengmei, a poor student who stayed in France. They were both deeply in love and vowed to form a good marriage.

Who knows that the sky is not as one wishes, and the environment is pressing. A certain old man used the authority of his father and brother to wrongly marry his daughter to his friend's family. Bai Wei vowed not to obey and was imprisoned by her father on the shore of West Lake. The woman committed suicide, but fortunately, she was rescued and did not succeed. Bai Wei hid her name and made up her mind to become an unprecedented living corpse. The father saw the suicide note and regretted it. He loved his daughter and hated her, and was overwhelmed with grief. He ordered the servant to open another room as a place for the woman to rest her soul, providing three meals a day to worship, and arranging the bed and quilt at night, and erected his beloved daughter's tomb on the shore of the lake, in order to pay tribute.

Days and months passed, and three years passed in an instant. Yang Sheng took his younger brother to Hangzhou for sightseeing, and happened to stay in a quiet room at night. Mengmei was writing by the light of the lamp, and vaguely heard the weeping of a resentful woman. Yang Sheng was curious, so he followed the sound.

As soon as Mengmei came out, Bai Wei entered. She happened to see Yang's younger brother sleeping soundly, and the woman was shocked and wanted to retreat. She caught a glimpse of the manuscript on the table, held it and recited it, sometimes sad and sometimes happy. Suddenly, sorrow came from her heart, because she was reading Yang Sheng's tearful history. Then she inquired about Yang's younger brother, and learned that Mengmei was forced to marry, but still missed Bai Wei. The woman secretly thought that her ambition was in vain, so she used a plan to escape.

When Mengmei returned, his younger brother told him, so the brothers searched everywhere, and they only found her when they heard the gunshot. Yang Sheng was overjoyed, but who knew that the woman died soon after. Alas, the sky did not bless her, and they only met for the last time. Mengmei was too stimulated, and his illness broke out and he coughed up blood and died. Alas, the tragedy on the lake is the fault of stubbornness.

Ballad Singing 229

Lu Qiuxia's Double Pearl Phoenix

Zhongxi (1040) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening Chapter "Plum Blossom Snow"

Plum blossoms are just blooming and snow is piling up. Plum blossoms in the snow are even brighter. Without snow, the plum blossoms lack charm. Without plum blossoms, the snow lacks interest. The fragrance of plum blossoms carries a smile and the snow floats cold. The snow reflects the plum blossoms and the plum blossoms accompany the snow. Snow is more pure and clean than plum blossoms. Plum blossoms can compete with snow to be the queen of flowers. The garden is open like snow. Playing in the snow can also be like exploring plum blossoms. The plum blossoms are determined to urge the end of winter. The snow melts and the plum blossoms bloom, calling for spring to come. Hao Ran steps on the snow to find plum blossoms. The snow embraces the inner boudoir and the flowers are blooming. Snow presses the plum blossoms and a high-ranking scholar lies down. Plum blossoms bloom on a snowy night and a beautiful woman comes. Watching the plum blossoms and admiring the snow makes the red sticky and warm. Plum blossoms and snow are both clear and pleasant. It can be said that snow and plum blossoms form a ring.

"Spring Flower" Character Chronicle 232

— Luo Gong

Gao Zhanfei resembles Shen Xiling's performance in "Boatman's Girl". He is still so strong and so enthusiastic. He is a very loyal character, but if someone is sorry for him, he will be just as sorry for others; anger is like an erupting volcano; he believes in the power of his own fist; when he is drunk, he is like a beast, and the beast wants to devour its enemies. In the tenderness and comfort, he is still as tame as a sheep! In the end, his rough throat vowed never to sing love songs again.

Yan Yuexian is a woman who follows gold, enjoying herself to the fullest, intoxicated to the fullest, and making gold angry to the fullest. However, she is also firmly cutting off her own destiny and destroying her own future. One day, when she realizes that gold has deceived her, the person who loves her loves someone else, and her own daughter scolds her for being a slave! Stop it? Die! How can death bury a body of sin?

Huang Naishuang: Wu Cun originally decided that this role would be played by Gao Qianping. Later, when Gao Qianping left, people were selected and it was discovered that Huang Naishuang was more suitable for playing this role. She sympathizes with Lao Gao, who has been stimulated, and in order to raise Lao Gao's son, she sacrificed her old father! But she does not complain about Lao Gao, she only encourages him to work hard and make progress!

Sun Min: This unfair society treats this bad guy too favorably. He doesn't really fall in love with people, he just wants to give people revenge! He only uses the stinky money that this stinky society gave him to subdue people. He never expected that the old man's fist was strong! He lay on the steps for a long sleep! It is still that corpse that should be imprisoned.

Zhu Qiuhen: Do you want to clearly understand the so-called "big star"? Come and see Zhu Qiuhen's performance! I'm worried that she will make people angry!

Wang Xianqi: You must be saying, "Bad guy"! That's right, that's enough to tell you!

Xie Yunqing: Holding two dull eyes, he is blind, but he said that this society is more blind than a blind person and cannot see the light!

Recent News from "The Thunder and Lightning Drama Society" 233

The "Thunder and Lightning Drama Society," which suddenly emerged in 1936, was certainly not accidental. It was the result of the efforts of several enthusiastic theater people to create this infant—the "Thunder and Lightning Drama Society."

They hold the greatest hope, dedicating all their spirit and strength to working hard in the theatrical movement, dropping a bomb on this thriving theatrical movement of 1936, giving the Chinese theater scene some new vitality!

Now they are focusing on internal construction because everything must be built firmly internally before it can begin to develop externally. Therefore, these two weeks have been spent on this construction work.

The first step of construction is: to elect Chen Lian as the leader to establish a council and jointly handle the affairs of the society, so all affairs are proceeding smoothly.

On the one hand, they are selecting scripts, preparing to start rehearsals. We will soon see the day their scripts are announced!

Cathay Screens "The Man Who Broke the Bank at Monte Carlo" 234

Cole Porter's Latest Starring Masterpiece

Produced by Twentieth Century Fox, starring Cole Porter, "The Man Who Broke the Bank at Monte Carlo" is being shown at the Cathay Grand Theatre starting today (Saturday). The opening scene of the film takes place in a famous club in Monte Carlo. Porter plays a desperate Western European Russian duke who stakes all his savings on a single gamble at the casino. He wins millions of francs and becomes a millionaire overnight, but later, because of a woman, he loses all the money he won, but the woman falls in love with him. This is a work that best suits Porter's personality. The female supporting role is the famous Joan Bennett. The film features gorgeous scenery in Monte Carlo and Paris, as well as the elegant scenery of the snowy mountains in Switzerland.
